%\tagged{Ans@MC, Type@Concept, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Theorems-IVT, File@0005}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0005. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Intermediate Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{4 \, {\left(x - 1\right)}^{\frac{1}{7}} - 3}\; , & x<{2}\\[3pt]
{7 \, {\left(x - 1\right)}^{\frac{1}{7}} - 6}\; , & x\geq{2}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-7},{10}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0005. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Intermediate Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{6 \, {\left(x - 3\right)}^{3} - 4}\; , & x<{4}\\[3pt]
{10 \, {\left(x - 3\right)}^{\frac{1}{3}} - 8}\; , & x\geq{4}
\end{array}\right.\]

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

{4 \cdot 2^{x - 5} - 4}\; , & x<{5}\\[3pt]
{9 \, e^{\left(x - 5\right)} - 9}\; , & x\geq{5}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{3},{13}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-4},{7}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

Does the Intermediate Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{7 \cdot 5^{x - 1} - 3}\; , & x<{1}\\[3pt]
{10 \, e^{\left(x - 1\right)} - 6}\; , & x\geq{1}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-2},{2}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

{6 \, x - 26}\; , & x<{5}\\[3pt]
{7 \, \log\left(x - 4\right) + 4}\; , & x\geq{5}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-2},{12}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0005. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Intermediate Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{4 \, {\left(x - 2\right)}^{\frac{1}{7}} - 1}\; , & x<{3}\\[3pt]
{{\left(x - 2\right)}^{\frac{1}{7}} + 2}\; , & x\geq{3}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-3},{13}]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0005.HELP.tex}

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice[correct]{Yes}
 \choice{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}
